    вЂў Exit 28 = TIMEOUT (--max-time 600s). The server did not finish
      sending a response before the limit.
    вЂў '0 bytes received' = curl got NO response body in that window (often
      stuck building a huge tools/list over SSE, or TCP hang).
    вЂў Try: export MCP_HTTP_CURL_TOOLS_LIST=300 (or higher), or give Docker
      more CPU/RAM; stdio tools/list can still PASS while HTTP is slow.
